msg:I am a bit disappointed with the service.

1) At the check-in, I was asked to fill out a temporary residence registration form, including private information about my work and activities in China. It is usually the document foreigners must fill out when they move to a new residence in China, but not at the hotel. It never happened in 7 years that I have lived in China.
When I asked the reason for filling out the document, I just got that it was the regulation...even though it is the only hotel where I was asked such a thing.
If it is a new regulation from today, I am ok to fill in, but we should be informed in advance of these requirements and not at the check-in.

2) The second issue is that services like indoor bars and lounges were closed, and we didn't get any reason for it when asking. The TRIP information about the hotel states that we should have access to these facilities. So either TRIP didn't update the hotel information, or the hotel didn't communicate about it.

msg:Do not book this Sofitel Galaxy when you come to Nanjing!
We brought our children to Nanjing to play on weekends. I booked a superior twin room. After checking into the room on the 35th floor around 11:00 p.m., I found the room was small and old. The TV was only about 21 inches. The old paint on the furniture was peeled off, and there was dust on the table. A star hotel is like a guest house, it is really not as good as a chain hotel, and it is seriously inconsistent with the grand and luxurious lobby. After we put forward our opinions to the front desk, we first said that there is no room tonight and we cannot change it, and that all the superior double rooms are like this, and we also admitted that the hotel has not been renovated for many years. After negotiating, we were finally changed to a deluxe twin room on the 30th floor. The room was much bigger (see photo). Although it was old, it was passable. It was almost 12 o'clock at this time.
The next night we went back to the hotel to take a bath and rest. My wife turned on the shower, and the water was cold. I thought the water would gradually heat up, but the water temperature was only a little bit hot during the whole process, but it was not at all the temperature for bathing. So My wife was shivering after washing. By the way, the supper sent by Ctrip took more than half an hour to arrive. It was said to be freshly made, but there was only a bowl of small wontons and two cakes, and the small wontons basically had no meat.
I reported the water temperature problem to the hotel, and I went to the Sun Yat-sen Mausoleum that day, and I was very tired and returned to the hotel without hot water, so I suddenly became angry. The manager on duty came up to test the water temperature, and it was true that the water temperature was not too hot. The manager's attitude was not bad, and he kept apologizing. But neither the child nor I have bathed yet. They said to change rooms, there was a suite available and we didn't because we had to pack our bags. The duty manager suggested that we go to the suite on the 40th floor to take a shower and then come down after the shower. My wife got a heater so I went up to the 40th floor with toiletries and a change of clothes, the suite was just as old, with dust on the glass and table tops. My son and I both took a shower and took a break. It was past 12 o'clock and we were too tired. Check out the room the next day and leave the hotel.
This is the most wonderful experience. When you stay in a five-star hotel, you actually take a towel and go to other rooms to take a shower, just like the guest house in the 1970s. It's a shame, it's a shame for the Accor Group, a global Sofitel, and Nanjing. The hotel was willing to compensate us. At the beginning, it was a 68 yuan noon buffet voucher (it was proposed at 10:30, and we had just finished breakfast). Besides, we had to leave Nanjing in the afternoon. After their internal discussion, it was changed to a 20% discount on the room rate. Based on the attitude of the hotel's superiors squeezing toothpaste, I did not accept the 20% discount. In the end, the compensation plan they gave was to reduce the room fee for one night.
Dear friends from Ctrip, even if I accept a certain compensation, I still want to remind you who are looking at this hotel, be careful!
However, I have to say that Ctrip's customer service has been helping me communicate with the hotel throughout the process, thank you very much.
